<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">грьчьскъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">grĭčĭskŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грецкий.html>гре́цкий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gréckij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грек.html>грек</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">grek</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-еский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-eskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>Greek</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:греча.html>гре́ча</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gréča</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:грешить.html>греши́ть</a> (16288)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грешить.html>греши́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">grešítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:согрешить.html>согреши́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sin <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to commit a sin</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грех.html>грех</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">grex</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грешный.html>гре́шный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gréšnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)грешне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)грешне́й</b>)

<ol><li>sinful</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> short form only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> guilty, culpable</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гриб.html>гриб</a> (1841)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gribъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гриб.html>гриб</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">grib</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гриб.html>гриба́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гриб.html>грибы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гриб.html>грибо́в</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гривна.html>гри́вна</a> (23494)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грива.html>гри́ва</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gríva</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mane, neck</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, derived from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*griva</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гривна.html>гри́вна</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">grívna</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гривна.html>гри́вны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гривна.html>гри́вны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гривна.html>гри́вен</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> grivna '<span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">unit of currency and weight in in medieval Rus</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гримаса.html>грима́са</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">grimása</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гримаса.html>грима́сы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гримаса.html>грима́сы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гримаса.html>грима́с</a></b>)

***гроб.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гроб.html>гроб</a> (2252)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*grobъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гроб.html>гроб</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">grob</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гроб.html>гро́ба</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гроб.html>гробы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гроб.html>гробо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>coffin</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> grave
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вогнать.html>вогна́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:гроб.html>гроб</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vognátʹ v <b>grob</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to drive to the grave</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:гроб.html>гро́ба</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:гроб.html>гроб</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жи́зни</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">do <b>gróba</b>, po <b>grob</b> žízni</i> ― <span class="e-translation">until death, as long as one shall live</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:могила.html>моги́ла</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mogíla</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***гробовой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гробовой.html>гробово́й</a> (13825)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гроб.html>гроб</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">grob</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ово́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гробовой.html>гробово́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">grobovój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> coffin
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:гробовой.html>гробово́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:портрет.html>портре́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>grobovój</b> portrét</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/coffin_portrait" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:coffin portrait"><b>coffin</b> portrait</a></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sepulchral, deathly
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:гробовой.html>гробово́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:голос.html>го́лос</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>grobovój</b> gólos</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>sepulchral</b> voice</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:гробовой.html>гробово́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:молчание.html>молча́ние</a>; <b><a href = vnd.unilang:гробовой.html>гробова́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тишина.html>тишина́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>grobovóje</b> molčánije; <b>grobovája</b> tišiná</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>deathly</b> silence/hush</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:гробовой.html>гробово́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:доска.html>доски́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">do <b>grobovój</b> doskí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">till one's dying day; as long as one lives</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">till the <b>deathly</b> plank</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гроб.html>гроб</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">grob</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:гроза.html>гроза́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">groza</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">horror</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*groza</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гроза.html>гроза́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">grozá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гроза.html>грозы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гроза.html>гро́зы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гроза.html>гроз</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гроздь.html>гроздь</a> (23725)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*grozdъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гроздь.html>гроздь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">grozdʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гроздь.html>гро́зди</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гроздь.html>гро́здья</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гроздь.html>гро́зди</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гроздь.html>гро́здьев</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гроздь.html>грозде́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bunch, cluster <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a group of a number of similar things</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:гроздь.html>гро́здья</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:виноград.html>виногра́да</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>grózdʹja</b> vinográda</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>bunches</b> of grapes</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***грозить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:грозить.html>грози́ть</a> (2849)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*groziti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грозить.html>грози́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">grozítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:погрозить.html>погрози́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пригрозить.html>пригрози́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to threaten</li>
<li>to make threatening gestures</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be in danger of, to face
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:грозить.html>грози́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:банкротство.html>банкро́тство</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jemú <b>grozít</b> bankrótstvo.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He is facing bankruptcy.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грозить.html>грози́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">grozítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
